Grand Prix Trial Winning Decklists
==================================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on April 16, 2016 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/henke_author.jpg)
By Tobi Henke











Before the Grand Prix itself come the Grand Prix Trials. As is tradition, on Friday, players had their final chance to enter into these tournaments, win five rounds, and earn two byes for the weekend's main event. Not only do those byes come in handy, since *Shadows over Innistrad* had only been for sale for a week by now, many players could also use the opportunity to get in a little more practice with the brand new Sealed Deck format.


The following decks were all piloted to victory by their respective pilots. Their lists provide an early idea of what to expect on Day 1 of Grand Prix Barcelona.







#### Carlos Gurmanies, Grand Prix Trial Winner


##### 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
